d/dx (7*x**2 + 9*x - 3) = 14*x + 9
∫ (-7*x**2 - 4*x - 5) dx = -7*x**3/3 - 2*x**2 - 5*x + C
∫ (-2*x**3 - 10*x**2 + 9*x - 5) dx = -x**4/2 - 10*x**3/3 + 9*x**2/2 - 5*x + C
d/dx (-8*x**3 + 9*x**2 + 3*x + 3) = -24*x**2 + 18*x + 3
∫ (9*x**3 - x**2 + 7) dx = 9*x**4/4 - x**3/3 + 7*x + C
∫ (6*x - 1) dx = 3*x**2 - x + C
∫ (-4*x**3 + 3*x**2 + 8*x - 4) dx = -x**4 + x**3 + 4*x**2 - 4*x + C
∫ (x*(-9*x - 7)) dx = -3*x**3 - 7*x**2/2 + C
∫ (-9*x**2 + 7*x + 5) dx = -3*x**3 + 7*x**2/2 + 5*x + C
∫ (6*x**3 - 4*x**2 + 10*x - 7) dx = 3*x**4/2 - 4*x**3/3 + 5*x**2 - 7*x + C
∫ (8*x**3 - 5*x**2 - 7*x - 1) dx = 2*x**4 - 5*x**3/3 - 7*x**2/2 - x + C
∫ (7*x**2 + 8) dx = 7*x**3/3 + 8*x + C
d/dx (7*x**2 + 5*x + 7) = 14*x + 5
∫ (8*x**3 - 5*x**2 + 8*x - 10) dx = 2*x**4 - 5*x**3/3 + 4*x**2 - 10*x + C
d/dx (3*x + 5) = 3
∫ (4*x + 6) dx = 2*x**2 + 6*x + C
d/dx (10*x**2 + 5*x - 6) = 20*x + 5
∫ (8*x**3 + 6*x**2 - 5*x + 8) dx = 2*x**4 + 2*x**3 - 5*x**2/2 + 8*x + C
∫ (8*x - 5) dx = 4*x**2 - 5*x + C
d/dx (-4*x**2 + 6*x + 3) = 6 - 8*x
∫ (-9*x**2 - 3*x + 1) dx = -3*x**3 - 3*x**2/2 + x + C
∫ (10*x**3 + 4*x - 5) dx = 5*x**4/2 + 2*x**2 - 5*x + C
d/dx (2*x**2 + 7*x + 8) = 4*x + 7
d/dx (8*x**2 - 8*x + 1) = 16*x - 8
∫ (-3*x**3 - 4*x**2 - 8*x - 5) dx = -3*x**4/4 - 4*x**3/3 - 4*x**2 - 5*x + C
d/dx (-5*x**2 + x - 7) = 1 - 10*x
d/dx (2 - 7*x) = -7
d/dx (10*x**2 + 8*x - 2) = 20*x + 8
∫ (x**2 + 5*x + 3) dx = x**3/3 + 5*x**2/2 + 3*x + C
d/dx (3*x + 7) = 3
∫ (8*x**3 - 6*x**2 + 8*x - 1) dx = 2*x**4 - 2*x**3 + 4*x**2 - x + C
∫ (3*x - 8) dx = 3*x**2/2 - 8*x + C
d/dx (3 - 8*x) = -8
d/dx (-3*x**2 - 2*x + 2) = -6*x - 2
d/dx (4*x**3 + 2*x**2 - 4*x - 5) = 12*x**2 + 4*x - 4
d/dx (x*(9 - 5*x**2)) = 9 - 15*x**2
∫ (2*x - 6) dx = x**2 - 6*x + C
d/dx (10*x + 6) = 10
∫ (7*x**3 - 4*x**2 - 2*x - 10) dx = 7*x**4/4 - 4*x**3/3 - x**2 - 10*x + C
∫ (-7*x**2 + 7*x - 10) dx = -7*x**3/3 + 7*x**2/2 - 10*x + C
d/dx (8*x - 8) = 8
d/dx (-10*x**2 - 10) = -20*x
∫ (6*x**2 - 6*x - 3) dx = 2*x**3 - 3*x**2 - 3*x + C
d/dx (5*x**3 + 5*x**2 - 8*x - 8) = 15*x**2 + 10*x - 8
∫ (2*x**3 + 3*x**2 + 8*x - 1) dx = x**4/2 + x**3 + 4*x**2 - x + C
∫ (5*x**2 - 7*x + 5) dx = 5*x**3/3 - 7*x**2/2 + 5*x + C
∫ (3*x - 5) dx = 3*x**2/2 - 5*x + C
∫ (-3*x**2 - 7*x + 8) dx = -x**3 - 7*x**2/2 + 8*x + C
d/dx (-7*x**2 - 3*x - 3) = -14*x - 3
d/dx (-6*x**2 + 2*x + 4) = 2 - 12*x
∫ (8*x**3 - 7*x**2 + x + 6) dx = 2*x**4 - 7*x**3/3 + x**2/2 + 6*x + C
∫ (9*x**2 - 9*x + 10) dx = 3*x**3 - 9*x**2/2 + 10*x + C
∫ (10*x**2 + 5*x - 3) dx = 10*x**3/3 + 5*x**2/2 - 3*x + C
d/dx (-4*x**2 + 8*x - 3) = 8 - 8*x
∫ (3*x**2 - 5*x + 10) dx = x**3 - 5*x**2/2 + 10*x + C
d/dx (-9*x**2 - 9*x - 9) = -18*x - 9
∫ (-2*x**3 + 8*x**2 + x - 4) dx = -x**4/2 + 8*x**3/3 + x**2/2 - 4*x + C
d/dx (8*x - 1) = 8
d/dx (-3*x**2 + 9*x - 2) = 9 - 6*x
∫ (2*x - 9) dx = x**2 - 9*x + C
∫ (9 - 8*x**2) dx = -8*x**3/3 + 9*x + C
∫ (-3*x**3 - 4*x**2 - 9*x + 6) dx = -3*x**4/4 - 4*x**3/3 - 9*x**2/2 + 6*x + C
∫ (4*x**3 + 9*x**2 - 4*x + 4) dx = x**4 + 3*x**3 - 2*x**2 + 4*x + C
d/dx (5*x + 10) = 5
d/dx (x + 9) = 1
∫ (x**3 + 4*x**2 + 9*x - 3) dx = x**4/4 + 4*x**3/3 + 9*x**2/2 - 3*x + C
d/dx (-10*x**2 - 7*x - 7) = -20*x - 7
∫ (-10*x**3 - 5*x**2 - 7*x + 8) dx = -5*x**4/2 - 5*x**3/3 - 7*x**2/2 + 8*x + C
d/dx (4 - 9*x) = -9
∫ (-2*x**2 + 9*x + 4) dx = -2*x**3/3 + 9*x**2/2 + 4*x + C
∫ (7*x**2 + 2*x + 6) dx = 7*x**3/3 + x**2 + 6*x + C
d/dx (-4*x**2 + 7*x + 2) = 7 - 8*x
∫ (-10*x**2 + 3*x - 6) dx = -10*x**3/3 + 3*x**2/2 - 6*x + C
d/dx (8*x**2 + 4*x - 6) = 16*x + 4
∫ (10*x - 10) dx = 5*x**2 - 10*x + C
d/dx (6*x**3 - 2*x**2 - 9*x - 2) = 18*x**2 - 4*x - 9
d/dx (2*x - 2) = 2
∫ (-9*x**3 + 6*x**2 + 2*x - 5) dx = -9*x**4/4 + 2*x**3 + x**2 - 5*x + C
d/dx (-7*x**3 - 9*x**2 + 9*x + 7) = -21*x**2 - 18*x + 9
∫ (10*x + 2) dx = 5*x**2 + 2*x + C
d/dx (x*(-10*x**2 + 5*x - 1)) = -10*x**2 + x*(5 - 20*x) + 5*x - 1
d/dx (7*x + 1) = 7
d/dx (x**2*(5*x + 7)) = 5*x**2 + 2*x*(5*x + 7)
d/dx (-3*x**3 + 7*x**2 - 4*x - 6) = -9*x**2 + 14*x - 4
d/dx (-10*x - 9) = -10
∫ (-4*x**3 - 3*x**2 - 4*x + 8) dx = -x**4 - x**3 - 2*x**2 + 8*x + C
